# Q : What is the main merits and demerits of Dependency Injection ?

**Dependency Injection (DI)** ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£ **merits** ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **demerits** ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶≤‡¶æ‡ßü ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶õ‡¶ø‡•§

---

## ‚úÖ **Main Merits (‡¶∏‡ßÅ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶ß‡¶æ)** of Dependency Injection

| ‡¶∏‡ßÅ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶ß‡¶æ                      | ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ                                                                                  |
| --------------------------- | ----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| **1. Loosely Coupled Code** | ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶∏‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶è‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ö‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ì‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶Æ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶≠‡¶∞‡¶∂‡ßÄ‡¶≤ ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá, ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶®‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ì ‡¶ü‡ßá‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§            |
| **2. Better Testability**   | ‡¶Æ‡¶ï (Mock) ‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶´‡ßá‡¶ï (Fake) ‡¶°‡¶ø‡¶™‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶°‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶∏‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶á ‡¶á‡¶û‡ßç‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü, ‡¶´‡¶≤‡ßá Unit Testing ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§     |
| **3. Code Reusability**     | ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü responsibility ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡ßÄ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶∏ ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶π‡ßü, ‡¶´‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶ú‡¶æ‡ßü‡¶ó‡¶æ‡ßü ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§        |
| **4. Flexibility**          | ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶∏ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá, ‡¶§‡¶æ ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßã‡¶≤ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø (e.g., service bind)‡•§ |
| **5. Maintainability**      | ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶° ‡¶Æ‡¶°‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶π‡ßü, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶á ‡¶è‡¶ï ‡¶ú‡¶æ‡ßü‡¶ó‡¶æ‡ßü ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ú‡¶æ‡ßü‡¶ó‡¶æ‡ßü ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§                      |

---

## ‚ùå **Main Demerits (‡¶Ö‡¶∏‡ßÅ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶ß‡¶æ)** of Dependency Injection

| ‡¶Ö‡¶∏‡ßÅ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶ß‡¶æ                                      | ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ                                                                      |
| -------------------------------------------- | ----------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| **1. Complexity for Beginners**              | ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶® ‡¶°‡ßá‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶≤‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø DI ‡¶ì Service Container ‡¶¨‡ßÅ‡¶ù‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶ú‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶≤ ‡¶π‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§      |
| **2. Debugging Difficulty**                  | ‡¶Ö‡¶ü‡ßã-‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶ú‡¶≤‡ßç‡¶≠ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® ‡¶°‡¶ø‡¶™‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶°‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶∏‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶•‡¶æ ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶ü‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∏ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶†‡¶ø‡¶® ‡¶π‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ |
| **3. Overhead in Small Projects**            | ‡¶õ‡ßã‡¶ü ‡¶Ö‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø DI setup ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ï ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßü ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡ßú‡¶§‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶§‡ßã ‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶ó‡ßá‡•§               |
| **4. Performance (‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶ó‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶∞‡ßá bind ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá)** | ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ï ‡¶°‡¶ø‡¶™‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶°‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶∏‡¶ø ‡¶ì binding ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶´‡¶∞‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶∏ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡ßÅ ‡¶ï‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá (rare)‡•§  |

---

## üéØ ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶™‡ßá ‡¶Æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßå‡¶∂‡¶≤:

| ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶ï        | ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶æ                                             |
| ---------- | ------------------------------------------------- |
| üëç ‡¶∏‡ßÅ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶ß‡¶æ  | Maintainable, Testable, Flexible, Loosely Coupled |
| üëé ‡¶Ö‡¶∏‡ßÅ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶ß‡¶æ | ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶ú‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶≤, Debug ‡¶ï‡¶†‡¶ø‡¶®, ‡¶õ‡ßã‡¶ü ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡ßá ‡¶Ö‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßü‡ßã‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßÄ‡ßü |

---

### ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶≤‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ó‡ßá‡¶≤‡ßá:

**Without DI:**

```php
class A {
    protected $b;
    public function __construct() {
        $this->b = new B(); // Hard-coded dependency
    }
}
```

**With DI:**

```php
class A {
    public function __construct(B $b) {
        $this->b = $b; // Injected, easier to swap/test
    }
}
```

<br><div align="center"><strong>‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ ‚ú¶ x ‚ú¶ ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ</strong></div><br><br>


# Q : Is ORM first or Data abstraction layer first ?

‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡ßÅ‡¶ù‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶á ‚Äî **ORM (Object-Relational Mapping)** ‡¶Ü‡¶ó‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶ø **Data Abstraction Layer (DAL)**?

---


### ‚úÖ **Data Abstraction Layer (DAL):**

‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶§‡¶∞ (Layer) ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶Ö‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶®‡¶ï‡ßá SQL ‡¶¨‡¶æ Low-level DB details ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶æ ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡ßá‡•§

* ‡¶≤‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶Ø: Low-level query ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶æ abstraction ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ
* ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£: `DB::table('users')->where(...)` (Laravel's Query Builder)
* ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ORM ‡¶õ‡¶æ‡¶°‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶ì ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º

---

### ‚úÖ **ORM (Object-Relational Mapping):**

‡¶è‡¶ï ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡¶£‡ßá‡¶∞ DAL ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ ‡¶Ü‡¶∞‡ßã ‡¶â‡¶®‡ßç‡¶®‡¶§ ‡¶ì object-oriented ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø Database table ‡¶ï‡ßá Class ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç Row ‡¶ï‡ßá Object ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡ßü‡•§

* ‡¶≤‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶Ø: ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶∏-‡¶Ö‡¶¨‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶°‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶∏ ‡¶π‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶°‡ßá‡¶≤ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ
* ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£: `User::find(1)`, `$user->save()`

---

## üß≠ ‡¶â‡¶§‡ßç‡¶§‡¶∞:

### ‚ùó **‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶•‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá Data Abstraction Layer (DAL)**

‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶∞‡¶ì ‡¶â‡¶®‡ßç‡¶®‡¶§ ‡¶ì ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶π‡ßü ORM‡•§

---

## üï∞ ‡¶á‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∏:

| Layer | ‡¶Ü‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨               | ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ                                        |
| ----- | ---------------------- | ----------------------------------------------- |
| ‚úÖ DAL | ‡¶Ü‡¶ó‡ßá (Foundation Layer) | Raw query ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá abstraction ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá            |
| ‚úÖ ORM | ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßá (OOP enhancement)  | DAL-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶∏‡ßá object/class ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡ßü |

---

## ‚úÖ Laravel-‡¶è ‡¶è‡¶∞ Example:

| Layer | Laravel Example             | ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ                                     |
| ----- | --------------------------- | -------------------------------------------- |
| DAL   | `DB::table('users')->get()` | Query Builder, abstraction layer             |
| ORM   | `User::all()`               | Eloquent ORM, more elegant & object-oriented |

---

## üéØ ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶™‡ßá ‡¶Æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡ßã:

> **ORM is built on top of DAL.**
> ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡ßé, **DAL ‡¶Ü‡¶ó‡ßá, ORM ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§**

DAL ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø (foundation), ORM ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶Æ‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶Ü‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡¶¶‡¶æ‡ßü‡¶ï ‡¶ì structured building.

---

<br><div align="center"><strong>‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ ‚ú¶ x ‚ú¶ ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ</strong></div><br><br>


# Q : Explain about `hasMany`, `hasThrough` and `polymorphic` relationship.

Laravel-‡¶è Eloquent Relationship ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá **hasMany**, **hasManyThrough** ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **Polymorphic Relationship** ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ï ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡•§ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ï ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶≤‡¶æ‡ßü ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶õ‡¶ø ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶∏‡¶π, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶® ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßã‡¶ù‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§

---

### ‚úÖ 1. `hasOne` 

‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Æ‡¶°‡ßá‡¶≤ ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Æ‡¶°‡ßá‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶∞ **‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ instance** ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶§‡•§

#### ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£:

‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ú‡¶® **User** ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø **Phone** ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

```php
// User.php
public function phone()
{
    return $this->hasOne(Phone::class);
}
```

üëâ ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•: `users` ‡¶ü‡ßá‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø row ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá `phones` ‡¶ü‡ßá‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø row ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶§‡•§

---

## ‚úÖ 2. `hasMany` Relationship

### üß† ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ:

‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Æ‡¶°‡ßá‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ï‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶° ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Æ‡¶°‡ßá‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

**‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£:**
‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ú‡¶® **User** ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ï‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã **Post** ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

### üîß ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶°:

**User.php**

```php
public function posts() {
    return $this->hasMany(Post::class);
}
```

**Post.php**

```php
public function user() {
    return $this->belongsTo(User::class);
}
```

### üß™ ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞:

```php
$user = User::find(1);
$posts = $user->posts; // ‡¶ê ‡¶á‡¶â‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶¨ ‡¶™‡ßã‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ü
```

---

## ‚úÖ 3. `hasManyThrough` Relationship

### üß† ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ:

‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Æ‡¶°‡ßá‡¶≤ ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ï‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶ü‡ßá‡¶° ‡¶Æ‡¶°‡ßá‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡ßÅ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶§, ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ù‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Æ‡¶°‡ßá‡¶≤ ‡¶∞‡ßü‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

> `hasManyThrough` ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶è‡¶Æ‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶® ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Æ‡¶°‡ßá‡¶≤ ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Æ‡¶°‡ßá‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá **‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßã‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá** ‡¶Ø‡ßÅ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÄ (intermediate) ‡¶Æ‡¶°‡ßá‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá‡•§


### üßæ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£ Scenario:

* ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø **Country**-‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ï **User** ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
* ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø **User** ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ï **Post** ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
* ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶á, ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø **Country** ‚Üí ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ï **Post** (‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá **User**)

### üìä ‡¶ö‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞:

```
Country 
   ‚Üì
 Users 
   ‚Üì
 Posts
```

---

### üóÉÔ∏è Database Structure:

| Table     | Columns                    |
| --------- | -------------------------- |
| countries | `id`, `name`               |
| users     | `id`, `name`, `country_id` |
| posts     | `id`, `title`, `user_id`   |

---

### üß© Implementation (Laravel):

#### ‚úÖ In `Country.php` Model:

```php
use Illuminate\Database\Eloquent\Model;

class Country extends Model {

    public function posts() {
        return $this->hasManyThrough(Post::class, User::class);
    }

    //or,

    public function posts() {
        return $this->hasManyThrough(
            Post::class,    // Final Model
            User::class,    // Intermediate Model
            'country_id',   // Foreign key on users table
            'user_id',      // Foreign key on posts table
            'id',           // Local key on countries table
            'id'            // Local key on users table
        );
    }
}
```

---

### üß™ ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ (Usage):

```php
$country = Country::find(1);
$posts = $country->posts;

foreach ($posts as $post) {
    echo $post->title . '<br>';
}
```

---

## ‚úÖ ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ (Laravel ‡¶ï‡ßÄ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá?):

Laravel ‡¶ï‡ßÄ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶á ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶°‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶§‡ßã SQL query ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶≤‡¶æ‡ßü:

```sql
SELECT posts.*
FROM posts
INNER JOIN users ON users.id = posts.user_id
WHERE users.country_id = 1
```

---




### ‚úÖ 4. `belongsTo` (‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßã ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶æ)

‡¶è‡¶á ‡¶Æ‡¶°‡ßá‡¶≤‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Æ‡¶°‡ßá‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶∞ **‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡ßã‡¶ù‡¶æ‡ßü**‡•§ ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡ßé current model ‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø model ‡¶ï‡ßá **belong ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá**‡•§

#### ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£:

‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø **Post** ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ú‡¶® **User** ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§

```php
// Post.php
public function user()
{
    return $this->belongsTo(User::class);
}
```
üëâ ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•: `posts` ‡¶ü‡ßá‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø row, `users` ‡¶ü‡ßá‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø row ‡¶ï‡ßá belong ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

---

### ‚úÖ 5. `belongsToMany` (‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ù‡ßá pivot table)

‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Æ‡¶°‡ßá‡¶≤ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶Ü‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Æ‡¶°‡ßá‡¶≤ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ö‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá **many-to-many** ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ï‡¶Ø‡ßÅ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶§‡•§ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ù‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø **pivot table** ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§

#### ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£:

‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ú‡¶® **User** ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ï **Role** ‡¶™‡ßá‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶Ü‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø **Role** ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ï **User** ‡¶™‡ßá‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

```php
// User.php
public function roles()
{
    return $this->belongsToMany(Role::class);
}

// Role.php
public function users()
{
    return $this->belongsToMany(User::class);
}
```

üëâ ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø `role_user` ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø pivot table ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§

---

## ‚úÖ 6. Polymorphic Relationship

### üß† ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ:

‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Æ‡¶°‡ßá‡¶≤ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶Æ‡¶°‡ßá‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ï ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶á structure ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá‡•§

**‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£:**
**Comment** ‡¶Æ‡¶°‡ßá‡¶≤ ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá ‚Äî ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ **Post**, **Video**, **Photo** ‚Äî ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶Æ‡¶°‡ßá‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶π‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

### üîß ‡¶ï‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶Æ‡¶°‡ßá‡¶≤:

**comments** ‡¶ü‡ßá‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶¨‡ßá `commentable_id` ‡¶ì `commentable_type` ‡¶´‡¶ø‡¶≤‡ßç‡¶°

**Comment.php**

```php
public function commentable() {
    return $this->morphTo();
}
```

**Post.php**

```php
public function comments() {
    return $this->morphMany(Comment::class, 'commentable');
}
```

**Video.php** (‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶á‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá)

```php
public function comments() {
    return $this->morphMany(Comment::class, 'commentable');
}
```

### üß™ ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞:

```php
$post = Post::find(1);
$comments = $post->comments;

$comment = Comment::find(1);
$relatedModel = $comment->commentable; // ‡¶π‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá Post, Video ‡¶¨‡¶æ Photo
```

---

## üìù ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶™‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶Ø:

| ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ï          | ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ                                  | ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£                     |
| ---------------- | ----------------------------------------- | -------------------------- |
| `hasMany`        | ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Æ‡¶°‡ßá‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶° ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶Æ‡¶°‡ßá‡¶≤‡ßá      | User ‚Üí Posts               |
| `hasManyThrough` | ‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Æ‡¶°‡ßá‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ù‡ßá ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÄ ‡¶Æ‡¶°‡ßá‡¶≤ ‡¶∞‡ßü‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá     | Country ‚Üí Users ‚Üí Posts    |
| `Polymorphic`    | ‡¶è‡¶ï ‡¶Æ‡¶°‡ßá‡¶≤ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶Æ‡¶°‡ßá‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡ßÅ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá | Comment ‚Üí Post/Video/Photo |

---


<br><div align="center"><strong>‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ ‚ú¶ x ‚ú¶ ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ</strong></div><br><br>


# Q : What is Route Model Binding ?


**Route Model Binding** ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá Laravel-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶´‡¶ø‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶∞, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ route parameter ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá **directly** ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø model instance ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‚Äî **Query ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá‡¶á manually**‡•§

---

## üî∏ ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡ßã ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡ßÄ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶Æ:

```php
Route::get('/users/{id}', function ($id) {
    $user = User::findOrFail($id);
    return $user;
});
```

‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá `$id` ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶ñ‡ßÅ‡¶Å‡¶ú‡ßá `User` ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá manually‡•§

---

## ‚úÖ Route Model Binding ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶á ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü:

```php
Route::get('/users/{user}', function (User $user) {
    return $user;
});
```

Laravel ‡¶¨‡ßÅ‡¶ù‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá `{user}` = `User` model ‡¶è‡¶∞ `id` ‡¶´‡¶ø‡¶≤‡ßç‡¶°‡•§
‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡ßé:

* `{user}` ‚Üí URL param
* `User $user` ‚Üí auto fetch by model

---

## üîç ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá?

Laravel internally ‡¶è‡¶á query ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶≤‡¶æ‡ßü:

```php
User::where('id', $user)->firstOrFail();
```

---

## üéØ ‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶á ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡¶£‡ßá‡¶∞ Binding ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá:

### 1. üîπ Implicit Binding (Default Laravel behavior)

**Route:**

```php
Route::get('/posts/{post}', function (Post $post) {
    return $post->title;
});
```

Laravel `id` ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá Post ‡¶ñ‡ßÅ‡¶Å‡¶ú‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡ßü‡•§

---

### 2. üî∏ Explicit Binding (custom column ‡¶¨‡¶æ logic)

**In `RouteServiceProvider`:**

```php
use App\Models\Post;

public function boot()
{
    Route::bind('post', function ($value) {
        return Post::where('slug', $value)->firstOrFail();
    });
}
```

**Then Route:**

```php
Route::get('/posts/{post}', function (Post $post) {
    return $post->title;
});
```

‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶® `/posts/laravel-tips` ‚Üí slug ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá Post ‡¶ñ‡ßÅ‡¶Å‡¶ú‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

---

## üß† ‡¶∏‡ßÅ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶ß‡¶æ (Merits of Route Model Binding):

| ‡¶∏‡ßÅ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶ß‡¶æ                 | ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ                                        |
| ---------------------- | ----------------------------------------------- |
| ‚úÖ Cleaner Code         | ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ `findOrFail()` ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡ßü ‡¶®‡¶æ               |
| ‚úÖ Automatic 404        | ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶ó‡ßá‡¶≤‡ßá `ModelNotFoundException` ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá 404 |
| ‚úÖ Type-Hinting Support | IDE/Editor auto-suggest ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá                     |
| ‚úÖ Security             | Only existing model accessible                  |

---

## üß™ Extra Example (with Controller):

```php
Route::get('/products/{product}', [ProductController::class, 'show']);
```

```php
public function show(Product $product) {
    return view('products.show', compact('product'));
}
```

---

## ‚úÖ ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶™‡ßá ‡¶Æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡ßã:

> Laravel automatically inject ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá Model instance based on the route parameter. ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶á Route Model Binding ‡¶¨‡¶≤‡ßá‡•§


<br><div align="center"><strong>‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ ‚ú¶ x ‚ú¶ ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ</strong></div><br><br>


# Q : If so many requests hit on a app, then how many instances are created ? One time or many times ?

Laravel ‡¶è ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ï‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã request ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶∏‡ßá, ‡¶§‡¶ñ‡¶® **‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø request ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶Ü‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶æ ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá Laravel ‡¶Ö‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ instance ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§** ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡ßé, **"‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø request = ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø Laravel application instance"**‡•§

### üîÑ ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶≤‡¶æ‡ßü:

Laravel ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø **stateless** ‡¶´‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ï ‚Äî ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø HTTP request ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü, ‡¶Ü‡¶ó‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® request ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá ‡¶Æ‡¶ø‡¶≤‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶®‡ßü‡•§

#### ‚úÖ ‡¶ï‡ßÄ ‡¶π‡ßü ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø Request ‡¶è?

1. **`public/index.php`** ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶•‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§
2. ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶™‡¶∞ Laravel ‡¶è‡¶∞ core (‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® service providers, middleware, routes ‡¶á‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶ø) bootstrapped ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§
3. ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø fresh **Application instance** ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§
4. Request ‡¶ü‡¶ø handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá response ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§
5. Response client ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡ßü ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶á instance destroy ‡¶π‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§

---

### üß† ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶∂‡ßç‡¶®:

**‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶á ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßü‡ßá ‡ßß‡ß¶‡ß¶‡ß¶‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶á‡¶â‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Ö‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶ø ‡ßß‡ß¶‡ß¶‡ß¶‡¶ü‡¶æ instance ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶π‡ßü?**

‚úîÔ∏è ‡¶π‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Å, Laravel ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø request ‡¶Ü‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá process ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶á **‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶§‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã concurrent request ‡¶Ü‡¶∏‡¶¨‡ßá, ‡¶§‡¶§‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá instance ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§** ‡¶§‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶á instance ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã **in-memory**, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç request ‡¶∂‡ßá‡¶∑ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶á destroy ‡¶π‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§

---

### üõ†Ô∏è ‡¶è‡¶á ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡ßá Laravel performance ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡ßú‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßü‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü:

* **Caching (config, route, view, query)**
* **Opcode cache (‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® OPcache)**
* **Queue system (‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® Job dispatching)**
* **Load balancer & horizontal scaling**
* **Optimized database queries & indexing**

---

### üîö ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶™‡ßá:

Laravel ‡¶è ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø request ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶Ü‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá instance ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ Laravel stateless ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø request ‡¶ï‡ßá independent ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§


<br><div align="center"><strong>‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ ‚ú¶ x ‚ú¶ ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ</strong></div><br><br>


# Q : What is Job-Queue ?

### ‚úÖ What is **Job-Queue** in Laravel?

**Job Queue** ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶è‡¶Æ‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ü‡ßá‡¶Æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ Laravel-‡¶è ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßü‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶™‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑ (slow or background) ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤ request ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá **‡¶™‡¶ø‡¶õ‡¶®‡ßá (background)** ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡ßÅ‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó ‡¶¶‡ßá‡ßü ‚Äî ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶Ö‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶® ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§ response ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

---

### üîÑ Simple Example:

üëâ ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡ßã, ‡¶á‡¶â‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶® ‡¶Ü‡¶™ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶§‡ßã‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø **Welcome Email** ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

* ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø ‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶Æ‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶á Email real-time-‡¶è ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶æ‡¶ì, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßã Email ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶∂‡ßá‡¶∑ ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶á‡¶â‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶∞ response ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ (‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶ó‡¶¨‡ßá)‡•§
* ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶á ‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶Æ‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶á Email ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú‡¶ü‡¶æ **Job Queue** ‡¶è ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶ì‡•§
* ‡¶á‡¶â‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶§‡¶ñ‡¶®‡¶á response ‡¶™‡¶æ‡ßü, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **queue worker** ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßá background-‡¶è email ‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§

---

### üîß Laravel Job Queue ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá?

1. **Job ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßã** ‚Üí ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶∏, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶Æ‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú‡¶ü‡¶æ define ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßã (‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶®: ‡¶á‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶á‡¶≤ ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã, report ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø, ‡¶á‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶ø)

   ```bash
   php artisan make:job SendWelcomeEmail
   ```

2. **Queue ‡¶§‡ßá Dispatch ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßã** ‚Üí

   ```php
   SendWelcomeEmail::dispatch($user);
   ```

3. **Queue worker ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶ì** ‚Üí

   ```bash
   php artisan queue:work
   ```

4. Laravel ‡¶è‡¶á Job ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã **Queue Driver** (‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® database, redis, Amazon SQS ‡¶á‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶ø) ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶® ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶∏ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

---

### üì¶ Common Use Cases:

| Use Case               | Why Use Queue?                 |
| ---------------------- | ------------------------------ |
| Email sending          | Delay-able, slow               |
| SMS sending            | Real-time ‡¶¶‡¶∞‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡ßá‡¶á            |
| Report generation      | Takes time                     |
| Image/video processing | CPU-intensive                  |
| Notifications          | Background execution is better |
| Payment processing     | Retry mechanism needed         |

---

### üîç Queue Drivers Laravel ‡¶è ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶™‡ßã‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá:

* `sync` (immediate, no actual queue)
* `database`
* `redis`
* `beanstalkd`
* `sqs` (Amazon)
* `rabbitmq` (3rd-party)

---

### üìå Benefits:

* Faster user experience
* Scalability (more workers = faster processing)
* Retry mechanism for failed jobs
* Error isolation (failed jobs don‚Äôt break the main app)

---

### üß† Summary:

Laravel ‡¶è‡¶∞ **Job Queue** system ‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤‡¶§ ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶ó‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶â‡¶®‡ßç‡¶°‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶∏ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Ö‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶®‡¶ï‡ßá responsive ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶¨‡ßú ‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßü‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶™‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑ task ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã efficiently ‡¶π‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶°‡¶≤ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

---

<br><div align="center"><strong>‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ ‚ú¶ x ‚ú¶ ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ</strong></div><br><br>


# Q : If I send 1000 mails or any operation using a chunk, then if any operation fails , then will the next operation continue or not ?

### üîç ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶∂‡ßç‡¶®:

Laravel ‡¶è ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶ø `chunk()` ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡ßß‡ß¶‡ß¶‡ß¶‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶á‡¶≤ ‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶Ö‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶ø, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Ö‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶® **‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶• (fail)** ‡¶π‡ßü ‚Äî ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶ø ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÄ ‡¶Ö‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶®‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßÅ ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶¨‡ßá?

---

### ‚úÖ ‡¶â‡¶§‡ßç‡¶§‡¶∞:

**‡¶π‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Å, ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§** Laravel-‡¶è‡¶∞ `chunk()` ‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶•‡¶° ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Ö‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶® ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶• ‡¶π‡ßü (‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶á‡¶≤ ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ó‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá exception ‡¶π‡ßü), ‡¶§‡¶¨‡ßÅ‡¶ì ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶ø ‡¶Ö‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶®‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶ö‡¶≤‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá ‚Äî ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶Æ‡¶ø ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ú‡ßá exception ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ß ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßã‡•§

---

### üß† ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶≤‡¶æ‡ßü:

```php
User::chunk(100, function ($users) {
    foreach ($users as $user) {
        Mail::to($user->email)->send(new WelcomeMail($user));
    }
});
```

‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶°‡ßá:

* `chunk(100)` ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø ‡ßß‡ß¶‡ß¶ ‡¶ú‡¶® ‡¶á‡¶â‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶∏ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§
* ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶è‡¶ï ‡¶á‡¶â‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶á‡¶≤ ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ó‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü (‡¶ß‡¶∞‡ßã network error), ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá Laravel ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶ø error ‡¶õ‡ßÅ‡¶Å‡ßú‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§
* ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø ‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶Æ‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶á error handle ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßã, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá `chunk()` ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ì‡¶á callback ‡¶¨‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ß ‡¶π‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÄ chunk ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶∏ ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§

---

### ‚ö†Ô∏è ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶á ‡¶ï‡ßÄ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá?

‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶Æ‡¶ø ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶ì ‡¶Ø‡ßá, **‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶á‡¶≤ ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶≠‡ßÅ‡¶≤ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶ì ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡¶¨ ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶® ‡¶†‡¶ø‡¶ï‡¶Æ‡¶§‡ßã ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü**, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá exception handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá:

```php
User::chunk(100, function ($users) {
    foreach ($users as $user) {
        try {
            Mail::to($user->email)->send(new WelcomeMail($user));
        } catch (\Exception $e) {
            \Log::error("Mail failed for {$user->email}: " . $e->getMessage());
            // Continue to next user
        }
    }
});
```

---

### üßæ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶™‡ßá:

| ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßü             | ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ                                                                          |
| ---------------- | --------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| Default ‡¶Ü‡¶ö‡¶∞‡¶£     | ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá error ‡¶π‡ßü ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶Æ‡¶ø exception ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡ßã, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶ì‡¶á chunk ‡¶¨‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ß ‡¶π‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ |
| Handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá      | ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø try-catch ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá exception ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡ßã, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶ø operations ‡¶ö‡¶≤‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§               |
| ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶∏ | Always use `try-catch` inside `foreach` when using `chunk()` for bulk tasks.      |

---

<br><div align="center"><strong>‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ ‚ú¶ x ‚ú¶ ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ</strong></div><br><br>


# Q : What is Laravel Throttle ?

**Laravel Throttle** ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø **rate limiting** ‡¶∏‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ü‡ßá‡¶Æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßÄ‡¶∞ **‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßü‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶ï request ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡ßÄ‡¶Æ‡¶æ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá**‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá Laravel ‡¶Ö‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶®‡¶ï‡ßá **spam, abuse ‡¶¨‡¶æ brute-force attack** ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§

---

### üì¶ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£:

‡¶ß‡¶∞‡ßã ‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶Æ‡¶ø ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶ì:

> ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø IP address ‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶á‡¶â‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø ‡ßß ‡¶Æ‡¶ø‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ü‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¨‡ßã‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶ö ‡ß´ ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ login ‡¶ö‡ßá‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶Æ‡¶ø Laravel Throttle middleware ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßã‡•§

---

### üîß ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá?

Laravel ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá `ThrottleRequests` middleware:

```php
Route::middleware('throttle:5,1')->post('/login', [AuthController::class, 'login']);
```

**throttle:5,1** ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá:

* ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø **‡ßß ‡¶Æ‡¶ø‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ü‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¨‡ßã‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶ö ‡ß´‡¶ü‡¶ø request** ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§
* ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶ø ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá Laravel response ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶¨‡ßá **429 Too Many Requests**‡•§

---

### üöÄ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶•‡¶æ‡ßü ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶π‡ßü?

| Use Case             | Purpose                   |
| -------------------- | ------------------------- |
| Login form           | Brute-force ‡¶Ü‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶Æ‡¶£ ‡¶†‡ßá‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã |
| Contact form         | Spam ‡¶ï‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã                |
| API endpoints        | Abuse/overuse ‡¶∞‡ßã‡¶ß ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ     |
| Search functionality | Server load ‡¶ï‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã         |

---

### üõ°Ô∏è Advanced Customization:

#### Custom throttle per user/IP:

```php
Route::middleware('throttle:10,1')->group(function () {
    Route::post('/api/search', 'SearchController@index');
});
```

#### Per route rate limit using `RateLimiter` (Laravel 8+):

```php
use Illuminate\Cache\RateLimiting\Limit;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\RateLimiter;

RateLimiter::for('login', function (Request $request) {
    return Limit::perMinute(5)->by($request->ip());
});
```

```php
Route::post('/login', [LoginController::class, 'store'])->middleware('throttle:login');
```

---

### üîÑ Behind the scenes:

Laravel internally uses **cache system** (like Redis, database, file) to store request count & timestamps.

---

### üìå Summary (‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶≤‡¶æ‡ßü):

* Laravel Throttle ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßü‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü request limit‡•§
* ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ö‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶Ö‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶ï request ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶≤‡¶ï ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶Ö‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶™‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§
* Throttle ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® `login`, `api`, ‡¶¨‡¶æ `search` ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶§‡ßã route-protect ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§

---

<br>

<div align="center"><strong>‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ ‚ú¶ x ‚ú¶ ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ</strong></div>

# Q : What is Collection ?

**Laravel Collection** ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã Laravel-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶∂‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶∂‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßÄ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶∏‡ßÅ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶ú‡¶®‡¶ï **data manipulation wrapper**, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤‡¶§ PHP array ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø `Illuminate\Support\Collection` ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶á‡¶®‡ßç‡¶∏‡¶ü‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶∏‡•§

> ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶≤‡¶≤‡ßá, **Collection** ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã array ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ì‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶ö‡¶Æ‡ßé‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞ object-oriented ‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶•‡¶°‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶π‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ü, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú‡ßá, ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶ì ‡¶ö‡ßá‡¶á‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶Ç ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶°‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶°‡ßá‡¶≤ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§

---

### ‚úÖ ‡¶ï‡¶¨‡ßá Collection ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶π‡ßü?

Eloquent query, `Model::all()`, `DB::table()->get()` ‡¶á‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞ Laravel **Collection ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§**

```php
$users = User::all();  // returns a Collection of User models
```

---

### üîß ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡ßü Collection ‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶•‡¶°:

| Method       | Description                             |
| ------------ | --------------------------------------- |
| `all()`      | ‡¶∏‡¶¨ ‡¶è‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü array ‡¶Ü‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá     |
| `pluck()`    | ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡ßÄ-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßÅ ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶®‡ßá |
| `map()`      | ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Ü‡¶á‡¶ü‡ßá‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡¶® ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßã‡¶ó ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá   |
| `filter()`   | ‡¶∂‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá |
| `first()`    | ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶•‡¶Æ ‡¶è‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá              |
| `where()`    | ‡¶∂‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡ßÄ ‡¶è‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶´‡¶ø‡¶≤‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá       |
| `contains()` | ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶§‡¶æ ‡¶ö‡ßá‡¶ï ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá        |
| `sum()`      | ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó‡¶´‡¶≤ ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá                   |
| `count()`    | ‡¶Æ‡ßã‡¶ü ‡¶Ü‡¶á‡¶ü‡ßá‡¶Æ ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá            |

---

### üß† ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£:

```php
$users = collect([
    ['name' => 'Irfan', 'age' => 25],
    ['name' => 'Nayeem', 'age' => 30],
]);

$filtered = $users->where('age', '>', 25);

// map example
$names = $users->pluck('name');  // ['Irfan', 'Nayeem']
```

---

### üÜö Collection vs Array

| Aspect    | Array                      | Collection                      |
| --------- | -------------------------- | ------------------------------- |
| Structure | Native PHP array           | `Illuminate\Support\Collection` |
| Syntax    | Procedural                 | Object-oriented + Chainable     |
| Features  | Limited built-in functions | 100+ expressive methods         |

---

### üìå ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞

Laravel Collection ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡ßü:

* **clean, readable, chainable** ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶° ‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡ßÅ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶ß‡¶æ
* **complex data transformation** ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶Æ‡¶§‡¶æ
* performance-friendly ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç testable ‡¶°‡¶ø‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶®

---

<br>

<div align="center"><strong>‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ ‚ú¶ x ‚ú¶ ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ</strong></div>

# Q : What is the purpose of using `.env` in a Laravel project ?

`.env` ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã Laravel ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡ßá‡¶∞ **environment configuration** ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡ßá‡¶∞ **‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶∏‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶≠ ‡¶ì ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶∂ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶≠‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶Ç‡¶∏** ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶®:

* ‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶§‡¶•‡ßç‡¶Ø (DB\_HOST, DB\_USERNAME, DB\_PASSWORD)
* ‡¶Ö‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ debug ‡¶Æ‡ßã‡¶° (APP\_DEBUG)
* ‡¶Ö‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ URL (APP\_URL)
* ‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶á‡¶≤ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶Ç‡¶∏
* API ‡¶ï‡ßÄ, ‡¶∏‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡ßÄ ‡¶á‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶ø

---

### `.env` ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∂‡ßç‡¶Ø:

1. **‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶∂ ‡¶Ü‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶æ ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶æ:**
   Development, Testing, Production‚Äî‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶æ environment ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶Ü‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶æ settings ‡¶¶‡¶∞‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡•§ `.env` ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤ ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶á ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶∂ ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡ßÄ ‡¶ï‡¶®‡¶´‡¶ø‡¶ó‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶® ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§

2. **‡¶∏‡¶ø‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶â‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡ßú‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã:**
   ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶∏‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶≠ ‡¶§‡¶•‡ßç‡¶Ø `.env` ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶°‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶∏ ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶æ ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶ó‡¶ø‡¶ü-‡¶è commit ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü (‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ `.env` ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶§ `.gitignore` ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá)‡•§

3. **‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶®‡¶´‡¶ø‡¶ó‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶® ‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ú‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü:**
   `.env` ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶Ö‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶Ç‡¶∏ ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶¶‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü, ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶° ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶õ‡ßÅ‡¶Å‡¶á‡ßü‡ßá‡¶á‡•§

---

### Laravel ‡¶è `.env` ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞:

Laravel ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßü `.env` ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶¨ environment variables `config` ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶° ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§
‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶°‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶®:

```php
env('DB_HOST', '127.0.0.1')
```

‡¶¨‡¶æ

```php
config('database.connections.mysql.host')
```

‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá `.env` ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶®‡•§

---

### ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶™:

* `.env` ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã environment specific ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶Ç‡¶∏ ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤
* ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Ö‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ **configurable ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶∏‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶ü ‡¶§‡¶•‡ßç‡¶Ø** ‡¶Ü‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶™‡¶¶‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá
* ‡¶°‡ßá‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶≤‡¶™‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßã‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶∂‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßü ‡¶ï‡¶®‡¶´‡¶ø‡¶ó‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶® ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶®‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶§‡ßã‡¶≤‡ßá
* `.env` ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤ ‡¶ó‡¶ø‡¶ü‡ßá ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü ‡¶®‡¶æ, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶∏‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶≠ ‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü

---

<div align="center"><strong>‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ ‚ú¶ x ‚ú¶ ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ</strong></div>

# Q : What is a polymorphic relationship in Eloquent? Can you give an example of its implementation?


## üß¨ **Polymorphic Relationship ‡¶ï‡ßÄ?**

Laravel Eloquent-‡¶è **Polymorphic Relationship** ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶è‡¶Æ‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø Relationship ‡¶∏‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ü‡ßá‡¶Æ, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Æ‡¶°‡ßá‡¶≤ **‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶Æ‡¶°‡ßá‡¶≤‡¶ï‡ßá** associate ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá **‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø common ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá**‡•§

> ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡ßé, ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶Æ‡¶® ‡¶ü‡ßá‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≤ (‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® `comments`) ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶ø `Post`, `Video`, `Image` ‡¶á‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶ø ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶Æ‡¶°‡ßá‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶ô‡ßç‡¶ó‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ï ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶™‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶®‡•§

---

## üß© ‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶® ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨?

‡¶ß‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶® ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá:

* Post ‡¶Æ‡¶°‡ßá‡¶≤
* Video ‡¶Æ‡¶°‡ßá‡¶≤
* ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç Comment ‡¶Æ‡¶°‡ßá‡¶≤

‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶ø ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø **Post** ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **Video**-‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§
‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶ø ‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶á‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶Ü‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶æ `post_comments` ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç `video_comments` ‡¶ü‡ßá‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≤ ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá‡¶®‡•§

‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ Laravel ‡¶è‡¶∞ **polymorphic relationship** ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ `comments` ‡¶ü‡ßá‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≤‡¶á ‡¶Ø‡¶•‡ßá‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‚Äî ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá‡¶á ‡¶∏‡¶¨ ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶¨‡ßÅ‡¶ù‡¶§‡ßá‡¶ì ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® ‡¶Æ‡¶°‡ßá‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶∞‡•§

---

## ‚úÖ **Laravel ‡¶è Polymorphic Relationship-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡¶®:**

1. üü° One-to-One Polymorphic
2. üü† One-to-Many Polymorphic ‚úÖ (‡¶∏‡¶¨‡¶ö‡ßá‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶ú‡¶®‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡ßü)
3. üîµ Many-to-Many Polymorphic

‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤‡¶§ **One-to-Many Polymorphic Relationship** ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨ ‚Äî Post/Video ‚Üí many Comments

---

## ‚úÖ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£: One-to-Many Polymorphic Relationship

### üî® Step 1: Comments ‡¶ü‡ßá‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶∞ Migration ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ

```php
Schema::create('comments', function (Blueprint $table) {
    $table->id();
    $table->text('content');
    $table->morphs('commentable'); 
    // ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶¨‡ßü‡¶Ç‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡ßü‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡ß®‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶Æ ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá:
    // 1. commentable_id
    // 2. commentable_type
    $table->timestamps();
});
```

**`commentable_id`** ‚Üí ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® ‡¶Æ‡¶°‡ßá‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶∞ ID
**`commentable_type`** ‚Üí ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® ‡¶Æ‡¶°‡ßá‡¶≤? Post ‡¶®‡¶æ Video?

---

### üì¶ Step 2: Model-‡¶è ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ï define ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ

#### üîπ Post ‡¶Æ‡¶°‡ßá‡¶≤ (Post.php)

```php
class Post extends Model
{
    public function comments()
    {
        return $this->morphMany(Comment::class, 'commentable');
    }
}
```

#### üîπ Video ‡¶Æ‡¶°‡ßá‡¶≤ (Video.php)

```php
class Video extends Model
{
    public function comments()
    {
        return $this->morphMany(Comment::class, 'commentable');
    }
}
```

#### üî∏ Comment ‡¶Æ‡¶°‡ßá‡¶≤ (Comment.php)

```php
class Comment extends Model
{
    public function commentable()
    {
        return $this->morphTo();
    }
}
```

üß† **‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ:**

* `Post` ‡¶ì `Video` ‡¶â‡¶≠‡ßü‡¶á **"commentable"** ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡ßá polymorphic relationship ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá
* `Comment` ‡¶Ü‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ `commentable` ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶® ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã parent (Post ‡¶¨‡¶æ Video) ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶ö‡¶ø‡¶®‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá

---

### üí¨ Step 3: ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶®?

#### A. ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø Post-‡¶è ‡¶ï‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶®:

```php
$post = Post::find(1);

$post->comments()->create([
    'content' => 'This is a comment on a post.'
]);
```

#### B. ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø Video-‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶®:

```php
$video = Video::find(1);

$video->comments()->create([
    'content' => 'This is a comment on a video.'
]);
```

#### C. Post ‡¶¨‡¶æ Video ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶¨ Comments ‡¶™‡ßú‡¶æ:

```php
$post = Post::find(1);
foreach ($post->comments as $comment) {
    echo $comment->content;
}

$video = Video::find(1);
foreach ($video->comments as $comment) {
    echo $comment->content;
}
```

#### D. Comment ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞ parent (Post/Video) ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ:

```php
$comment = Comment::find(1);
$parent = $comment->commentable; // ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá Post ‡¶¨‡¶æ Video

echo $parent->title;
```

---

## üîö ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞:

| ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßü                       | ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ                                                   |
| -------------------------- | ---------------------------------------------------------- |
| ‚úÖ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∂‡ßç‡¶Ø                 | ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶Æ‡¶°‡ßá‡¶≤‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶®/‡¶ü‡ßá‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶Ø‡ßÅ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ |
| ‚úÖ ‡¶∏‡ßÅ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶ß‡¶æ                   | ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶° ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶á‡¶â‡¶ú, ‡¶ï‡¶Æ ‡¶ü‡ßá‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≤, ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶® ‡¶°‡¶ø‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶®                          |
| ‚úÖ ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£ ‡¶ü‡ßá‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≤ ‡¶´‡¶ø‡¶≤‡ßç‡¶° | `commentable_id`, `commentable_type`                       |
| ‚úÖ ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶æ‡ßü‡¶ó‡¶æ          | Comment, Tag, Like, Attachment, Reaction ‡¶á‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶ø           |

---

## üß† ‡¶Æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶®:

* `morphs()` = ‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶á‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶´‡¶ø‡¶≤‡ßç‡¶° ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá (`*_id`, `*_type`)
* `morphTo()` = polymorphic relation ‡¶è‡¶∞ reverse
* ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶á pattern ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá Tag, Like, Image, Attachment ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ï ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶ì build ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§

---

<br>

<div align="center"><strong>‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ ‚ú¶ x ‚ú¶ ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ</strong></div>

# Q : How would you create and use a `Query Scope` in Laravel?

Laravel-‡¶è **Query Scope** ‡¶è‡¶Æ‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø powerful feature, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá Eloquent model-‡¶è reusable query logic ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶ú‡ßç‡¶û‡¶æ‡ßü‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡ßü‡•§

‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤‡¶§ Eloquent-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ **custom method** ‚Äî ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶ø ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶® query-‡¶§‡ßá‡•§

---

## üß© Query Scope ‡¶ï‡¶§ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞?

Laravel-‡¶è ‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶á ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ Query Scope ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá:

1. ‚úÖ **Local Scope** (‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá call ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü)
2. ‚úÖ **Global Scope** (‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶¨‡ßü‡¶Ç‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡ßü‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶¨ query-‡¶§‡ßá apply ‡¶π‡ßü)

---

## ‚úÖ Local Scope: ‡¶ï‡ßÄ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶®?

### üéØ Step 1: Model-‡¶è scope define ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶®

```php
// App\Models\Post.php

class Post extends Model
{
    // Local Scope
    public function scopePublished($query)
    {
        return $query->where('is_published', true);
    }
}
```

üîç ‡¶≤‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßã: scope method-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ **`scopePublished`**, ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ call ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßü ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ `published()` ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡¶¨‡•§

---

### üéØ Step 2: ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶®?

```php
$publishedPosts = Post::published()->get();
```

> ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶Æ‡¶® query ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá:
> `SELECT * FROM posts WHERE is_published = true`

---

### üß† ‡¶Ü‡¶∞‡¶ì ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£:

#### üîπ Active Users Scope

```php
// User.php

public function scopeActive($query)
{
    return $query->where('status', 'active');
}

// ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞
$activeUsers = User::active()->get();
```

#### üîπ Custom Parameter ‡¶∏‡¶π Scope

```php
// Product.php

public function scopePriceGreaterThan($query, $amount)
{
    return $query->where('price', '>', $amount);
}

// ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞
$expensiveProducts = Product::priceGreaterThan(1000)->get();
```

---

## ‚úÖ Global Scope (‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶™‡ßá)

‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶ø ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã condition ‡¶∏‡¶¨ query-‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶¨‡ßü‡¶Ç‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡ßü‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡ßÅ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶π‡ßã‡¶ï, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá **Global Scope** ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶®‡•§

```php
// App\Scopes\ActiveScope.php

class ActiveScope implements Scope
{
    public function apply(Builder $builder, Model $model)
    {
        $builder->where('status', 'active');
    }
}

// User.php model-‡¶è boot method ‡¶è
protected static function booted()
{
    static::addGlobalScope(new ActiveScope);
}
```

‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶® `User::all()` ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶¨‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßü `status = active` filter apply ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

---

## üß† ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶§‡¶æ:

| ‡¶∏‡ßÅ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶ß‡¶æ                | ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ                                     |
| --------------------- | -------------------------------------------- |
| üîÅ Reusable Query     | ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶á ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶° ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶¶‡¶∞‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡ßá‡¶á               |
| üßº Clean Controller   | Controller ‡¶¨‡¶æ Repository ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶° ‡¶õ‡ßã‡¶ü ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü    |
| üîí DRY Principle      | DRY (Don't Repeat Yourself) ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü         |
| üìä Parametrized Scope | Dynamic value support ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá (price, date etc.) |

---

## ‚úÖ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞:

| ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡¶£            | ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú                                                |
| -------------- | -------------------------------------------------- |
| `scopeXyz`     | Local Scope method                                 |
| `Model::xyz()` | Scope call                                         |
| Reusability    | High                                               |
| Use-case       | Common filters (published, active, verified, etc.) |

---


<br>

<div align="center"><strong>‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ ‚ú¶ x ‚ú¶ ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ</strong></div>

# Q : What is the difference between `queue` and `event` in Laravel? Can you provide a use case for each?


Laravel-‡¶è **Queue** ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **Event** ‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶ü‡ßã‡¶á ‡¶Ü‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶ì, ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ï ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßü ‡¶è‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú‡¶ì ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶ü‡ßã‡¶á **asynchronous operation** ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡ßü, ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡¶®, ‡¶â‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∂‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ì ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶ß‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶∞‡ßü‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

---

## üß© ‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤ ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶Ø: Queue vs Event

| ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßü               | Queue                                 | Event                                                            |
| ------------------ | ------------------------------------- | ---------------------------------------------------------------- |
| ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú                | Delayed ‡¶¨‡¶æ background task handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá | ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ trigger-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï ‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶ø‡¶ï listener ‡¶ï‡ßá notify ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá |
| Execution Time     | ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßá execute ‡¶π‡ßü (job dispatch ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá)    | ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá listener trigger ‡¶π‡ßü                                    |
| Primary Purpose    | Time-consuming task ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã delay ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ    | Loose coupling ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç action trigger ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ                            |
| Laravel Class      | `Job` class                           | `Event` ‡¶ì `Listener` class                                       |
| Queue ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá? | ‡¶Ö‡¶¨‡¶∂‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶á                                | ‡¶á‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá queue-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡ßÅ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü                           |
| ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£             | Email ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã, report generate         | User registered ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá welcome mail ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã, audit log ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø          |

---

## ‚úÖ Queue - ‡¶ï‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßã?

‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶Æ‡¶ø ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶ì, ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú **immediate ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡ßá background-‡¶è ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßá** ‡¶ö‡¶≤‡ßÅ‡¶ï‡•§

### üìå Use Case: Email ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã

```php
// Controller ‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ì
SendWelcomeEmail::dispatch($user);
```

**Job Class:**

```php
class SendWelcomeEmail implements ShouldQueue {
    public function handle() {
        Mail::to($this->user->email)->send(new WelcomeMail($this->user));
    }
}
```

> ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá email ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã job queue ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßú‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá, real-time user delay ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§

---

## ‚úÖ Event - ‡¶ï‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßã?

‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶Æ‡¶ø ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶ì, ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ action trigger ‡¶π‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶ø‡¶ï response ‡¶π‡ßã‡¶ï, ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ loosely coupled ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

### üìå Use Case: User Registration

```php
// UserRegistered ‡¶á‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü fire ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ
event(new UserRegistered($user));
```

**Event Listener ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã:**

```php
class SendWelcomeNotification {
    public function handle(UserRegistered $event) {
        // Welcome Notification ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã
    }
}

class LogUserActivity {
    public function handle(UserRegistered $event) {
        // Activity Log ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ
    }
}
```

> ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá `UserRegistered` ‡¶á‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü fire ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá ‡ß®‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Ü‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶æ listener ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‚Äî ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá mail, ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá log‡•§

---

## üß† Event & Queue ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá?

Laravel-‡¶è Event ‡¶è‡¶∞ Listener ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶ì queue-‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§ ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡ßé ‚Äî

```php
class SendWelcomeNotification implements ShouldQueue
```

‡¶è‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶á‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü trigger ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶ì Listener background-‡¶è ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

---

## üß™ Summary Table:

| Aspect             | Queue                       | Event                           |
| ------------------ | --------------------------- | ------------------------------- |
| Purpose            | Background task             | Trigger-based multiple response |
| Delayable          | ‚úÖ                           | Depends                         |
| Queue Required     | ‚úÖ                           | Optional                        |
| Example            | Image resize, Email sending | UserRegistered, OrderPlaced     |
| Scalable           | ‚úÖ                           | ‚úÖ                               |
| Used with Listener | ‚ùå                           | ‚úÖ                               |

---

## ‚úÖ ‡¶ï‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßã?

* üëâ Long time ‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶ó‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶Æ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá ‚Üí **Queue**
* üëâ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã event ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶ø‡¶ï response ‡¶¶‡¶∞‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá ‚Üí **Event**
* üëâ Event + Job delay ‡¶¶‡¶∞‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá ‚Üí **Queueable Listener**

---

<br>

<div align="center"><strong>‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ ‚ú¶ x ‚ú¶ ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ</strong></div>

<br>
<br>

# Q : What is CSRF protection, and how does Laravel implement it?

**CSRF (Cross-Site Request Forgery)** ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø security vulnerability, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ú‡¶® attacker ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßÄ‡¶∞ ‡¶Ö‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶≤‡¶ó‡¶á‡¶® ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá malicious ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßã‡¶ß (request) ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

Laravel ‡¶è CSRF protection ‡¶ñ‡ßÅ‡¶¨‡¶á built-in ‡¶ì ‡¶∂‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶∂‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßÄ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§

---

## üõ°Ô∏è CSRF Protection ‡¶ï‡ßÄ?

**CSRF Attack**:
‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ attacker ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø ‡¶§‡ßã‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶∞ website-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã authenticated user ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Ö‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ request ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá (‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶®‡¶É form submit ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, data delete ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá), ‡¶§‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü CSRF attack‡•§

> üß† ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£: ‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶Æ‡¶ø ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶á site-‡¶è ‡¶≤‡¶ó‡¶á‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßã, attacker ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶á ‡¶≤‡¶ó‡¶á‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ session ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá backend ‡¶è request ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡ßü‡•§

---

## ‚úÖ Laravel ‡¶ï‡ßÄ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá CSRF ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá protect ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá?

Laravel ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø **POST, PUT, PATCH, DELETE** request-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø **CSRF Token** ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶æ‡ßü ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ verify ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

---

## üîê CSRF Token ‡¶ï‡ßÄ?

Laravel automatically generate ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø unique **token** ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø user session ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡•§

‡¶è‡¶á token:

* Form ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá hidden input ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá
* Server ‡¶è verify ‡¶π‡ßü
* Invalid ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá request reject ‡¶π‡ßü

---

## üìå Laravel form ‡¶è ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá token use ‡¶π‡ßü?

### Blade ‡¶è:

```blade
<form method="POST" action="/submit">
    @csrf
    <!-- form inputs -->
    <button type="submit">Submit</button>
</form>
```

üëâ `@csrf` ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶á ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá‡¶∞ HTML generate ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá:

```html
<input type="hidden" name="_token" value="lksjdf9023..." />
```

---

## üß™ Behind the Scene: Middleware

Laravel ‡¶è `VerifyCsrfToken` ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡ßá middleware ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ token validate ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá:

```php
// app/Http/Kernel.php
'web' middleware group ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá:
\Illuminate\Foundation\Http\Middleware\VerifyCsrfToken::class,
```

---

## üß† API route ‡¶è CSRF token ‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶ó‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶®?

* API routes (routes/api.php) typically use **token-based authentication (like Sanctum or Passport)**
* ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶á ‡¶è‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã CSRF exempted ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü

---

## ‚ùå ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø CSRF token ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü?

‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá Laravel ‡¶è‡¶á error ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá:

```
419 | Page Expired
```

---

## ‚úÖ Exclude route from CSRF (Not Recommended Unless Necessary)

```php
// app/Http/Middleware/VerifyCsrfToken.php
protected $except = [
    'payment/ipn-callback',
];
```

---

## üîí CSRF ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡ßÅ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶ß‡¶æ:

| Benefit                    | Description                                  |
| -------------------------- | -------------------------------------------- |
| ‚úÖ Secure Forms             | Form submission safe ‡¶π‡ßü                      |
| ‚úÖ Prevents Forged Requests | Authenticated user ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Ö‡¶™‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶†‡ßá‡¶ï‡¶æ‡ßü |
| ‚úÖ Session-bound token      | Per-user unique security                     |

---

## üéØ Summary:

* Laravel automatically CSRF token inject ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá
* Form-‡¶è `@csrf` ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶á ‡¶π‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü
* Middleware request verify ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá
* GET request exempted, POST, PUT, PATCH, DELETE request verify ‡¶π‡ßü

---

# Q : What are some strategies for optimizing a Laravel application‚Äôs performance?

‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ú‡¶® Laravel developer ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá performance optimization ‡¶ñ‡ßÅ‡¶¨ ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£ ‚Äî ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶® ‡¶Ö‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶™‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§ response ‡¶¶‡ßá‡ßü, scalable ‡¶π‡ßü, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç server load ‡¶ï‡¶Æ ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶á **Bangla-English mixed** explanation ‡¶§‡ßã‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ content ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßÅ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶∞‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç Markdown-compatible `--x--` ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶® ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã‡•§

---

## üöÄ 1. **Cache Routes, Views, and Configurations**

Laravel ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ app load ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßü route/config/view compile ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ Production environment-‡¶è ‡¶è‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶Ü‡¶ó‡ßá‡¶á compile ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá cache ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá load time ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ï ‡¶ï‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§

```bash
php artisan route:cache
php artisan config:cache
php artisan view:cache
```

üß† Debugging ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã clear ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßã:

```bash
php artisan route:clear
php artisan config:clear
php artisan view:clear
```


---

## ‚ö° 2. **Optimize Database Queries**

üîπ Eager Loading:

```php
$users = User::with('profile')->get(); // avoid N+1 problem
```

üîπ Indexing: `WHERE`, `JOIN`, `ORDER BY` ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶∏‡¶¨ column-‡¶è apply ‡¶π‡ßü, ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá database index ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶≤‡ßá query ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ï ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§ ‡¶ö‡¶≤‡ßá‡•§

üîπ Select Only Required Columns:

```php
User::select('id', 'name')->get(); // avoid SELECT *
```

üîπ Pagination:

```php
User::paginate(20); // Avoid loading 1000+ rows at once
```



---

## üîÅ 3. **Use Caching for Data**

Laravel ‡¶è‡¶∞ cache system ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá frequently-used data cache ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá performance boost ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§

üîπ Manual Cache:

```php
Cache::put('users', $users, now()->addMinutes(10));
```

üîπ Query Cache:

```php
$users = Cache::remember('users', 600, function () {
    return DB::table('users')->get();
});
```

üîπ Full Page Cache:
Static ‡¶¨‡¶æ rarely-changing page ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá full response cache ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßã‡•§



---

## üß∞ 4. **Optimize Autoloading**

Production-‡¶è unnecessary file load ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø optimized autoloading ‡¶¶‡¶∞‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡•§

```bash
composer install --optimize-autoloader --no-dev
```



---

## üåê 5. **Reduce HTTP Requests**

üîπ Laravel Mix ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá JS/CSS combine ‡¶ì minify ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßã:

```bash
npm run production
```

üîπ HTTP/2 server use ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßã (Nginx with HTTP/2 enabled) ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ï request handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§



---

## üì¨ 6. **Use Queues for Time-Consuming Tasks**

Email sending, file processing ‡¶á‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú queue ‡¶§‡ßá background ‡¶è ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶æ‡¶ì:

```php
dispatch(new SendEmailJob($user));
```

‚úÖ ‡¶è‡¶§‡ßá response ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§ ‡¶Ü‡¶∏‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç user wait ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§



---

## ‚öôÔ∏è 7. **Enable OPcache**

PHP script bytecode cache ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá OPcache ‚Äî ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá parsing time ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶Å‡¶ö‡ßá‡•§

üîß Enable it in `php.ini`:

```ini
opcache.enable=1
opcache.memory_consumption=128
opcache.validate_timestamps=0
```



---

## üåç 8. **Use a Content Delivery Network (CDN)**

Static assets ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® image, js, css ‚Äî ‡¶è‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã CDN ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá serve ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§ load ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§

* Cloudflare, BunnyCDN, AWS CloudFront use ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§



---

## üñºÔ∏è 9. **Compress and Optimize Images**

Laravel ‡¶è [Intervention Image](https://image.intervention.io/) use ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá image optimize ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßã‡•§

```php
$image = Image::make($request->file('image'))->resize(300, 200);
$image->save(public_path('optimized.jpg'));
```



---

## üíΩ 10. **Use a Faster Database (Where Possible)**

üîπ Redis/Memcached - session, queue, caching ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡•§

üîπ Query Breakdown - Complex multi-join query split ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá load-balanced result ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶ì‡•§



---

## üßµ 11. **Optimize Server and Deployment**

üîπ Use Nginx + PHP-FPM
üîπ Properly configure worker pool
üîπ Keep PHP, Laravel, and server software updated



## üì¶ 12. **Use HTTP Caching Headers**

```php
return response($content)
    ->header('Cache-Control', 'public, max-age=31536000');
```

Browser ‡¶è‡¶á asset ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ download ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá cache ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá load ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

---

## ‚úÖ Final Summary Table:

| Strategy                    | Description                 |
| --------------------------- | --------------------------- |
| üó∫Ô∏è Route/View/Config Cache | Compile ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá fast response   |
| üîé Eager Loading & Index    | DB query optimized          |
| üíæ Redis/Data Cache         | Reduce DB hits              |
| üì¨ Queues                   | Async background task       |
| üß† OPcache                  | Faster PHP execution        |
| üåê CDN & Image Optimization | Reduce asset size & latency |
| üíª Composer Optimize        | Lightweight deployment      |

---

# Q : How do you optimize large database queries in Laravel?

‡¶Ö‡¶¨‡¶∂‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶á! ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá Laravel-‡¶è **large database query optimization** ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø best practices ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã Bangla-English mix ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶∑‡¶æ‡ßü ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡ßü‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá interview ‡¶¨‡¶æ documentation ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶Æ‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßã‡•§

---

## ‚úÖ 1. Eager Loading ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá N+1 Problem Avoid ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ

```php
$posts = Post::with('comments')->get();
```

Laravel-‡¶è ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø ‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶Æ‡¶ø `with()` ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßã, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶æ post ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶Ü‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶æ ‡¶Ü‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá comment query execute ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá (‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶á N+1 problem ‡¶¨‡¶≤‡ßá)‡•§

Eager Loading ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá related model ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá load ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ performance boost ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

---

## ‚úÖ 2. ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßü‡ßã‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßÄ‡ßü Column ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã select() ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ

```php
$users = User::select('id', 'name', 'email')->get();
```

`SELECT *` ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶∏‡¶¨ column ‡¶¶‡¶∞‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡¶æ `select()` ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá query ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßã‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá query lightweight ‡¶π‡ßü ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶ï‡¶Æ data memory-‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶° ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§

---

## ‚úÖ 3. Pagination ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ

```php
$users = User::paginate(50);
```

‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶è ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá ‡ßß‡ß¶,‡ß¶‡ß¶‡ß¶ rows load ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá paginate ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡ß´‡ß¶‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá fetch ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá performance ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ï ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§

---

## ‚úÖ 4. Smart Where Clause ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ

```php
$users = User::where('status', 'active')->get();
```

Database ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶á filter ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶®‡ßã‡•§ Server-side filtering ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶ø memory ‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡ßü, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶á ‡¶Ø‡¶§‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶≠‡¶¨ SQL level-‡¶è filter ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßã‡•§

---

## ‚úÖ 5. Database Indexing

‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶∏‡¶¨ column-‡¶è frequently `where`, `join` ‡¶¨‡¶æ `orderBy` ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßã (‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶®: `email`, `user_id`, `status`) ‚Äì ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡¶æ‡ßü index apply ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßã‡•§

Indexing ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶≤‡ßá query ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡¶æ full table scan ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ slow ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡ßü‡•§

---

## ‚úÖ 6. Cache Query Result

```php
$users = Cache::remember('active_users', now()->addMinutes(10), function () {
    return User::where('status', 'active')->get();
});
```

bar bar ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶á query ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá database hit ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§ Cache ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ query ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶´‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶´‡¶≤ ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶ñ‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡ßü, ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÄ‡¶§‡ßá cache ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§

---

## ‚úÖ 7. Chunk ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá Large Dataset Process ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ

```php
User::chunk(100, function ($users) {
    foreach ($users as $user) {
        // process each user
    }
});
```

‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ï ‡¶¨‡ßú data load ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá memory overflow ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§ `chunk()` method data-‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶ó ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶ó ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

---

## ‚úÖ 8. Raw SQL query ‡¶è‡ßú‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá Query Builder/Eloquent ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ

Laravel ‡¶è‡¶∞ Query Builder ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç Eloquent ORM use ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá query safe ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç readable ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§ Try to avoid raw query unless absolutely needed.

---

## ‚úÖ 9. DB::listen() ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá Query Debug ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ

```php
DB::listen(function ($query) {
    logger($query->sql);
});
```

query ‡¶ï‡ßá analyze ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ use ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßã‡•§ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® query ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßü ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶æ slow perform ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶õ‡ßá ‚Äì ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

---

## ‚úÖ 10. Join ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ Multiple Query ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶æ‡ßü‡¶ó‡¶æ‡ßü

```php
$users = DB::table('users')
    ->join('orders', 'users.id', '=', 'orders.user_id')
    ->select('users.name', 'orders.total')
    ->get();
```

‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶ø‡¶ï query ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡ßá `join` ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§ data fetch ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç DB hit ‡¶ï‡¶Æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§

---

## ‚úÖ 11. DB Level Function ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ (count, sum, avg)

```php
$total = Order::where('status', 'paid')->sum('amount');
```

Laravel ‡¶è loop ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶¨ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßã DB function use ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® `count()`, `sum()`, `max()` etc.

---

## ‚úÖ 12. Eager Loading ‡¶è constraint apply ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ

```php
$posts = Post::with(['comments' => function ($query) {
    $query->where('approved', true);
}])->get();
```

Eager load ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶ì ‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶Æ‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá data fetch ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ filter ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßã‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá unapproved comment ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡¶æ avoid ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§

---

## ‚úÖ 13. Sorting ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßü index ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∂‡ßç‡¶ö‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ

```php
$users = User::orderBy('created_at', 'desc')->take(10)->get();
```

‡¶Ø‡ßá column ‡¶è sort ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá (`created_at`), ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ indexed ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶≤‡ßá sorting ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ï ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§

---

## ‚úÖ 14. Lazy Loading ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßü‡ßã‡¶ú‡¶® ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá use ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ

```php
foreach ($posts as $post) {
    $comments = $post->comments; // lazy loaded
}
```

‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡¶¨ post-‡¶è‡¶∞ comment ‡¶¶‡¶∞‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá lazy loading ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßã‡•§ ‡¶§‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßÅ‡¶ù‡ßá use ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá, ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá performance down ‡¶π‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

---

## ‚úÖ Bonus: EXPLAIN ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá Query Plan Check ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ

```sql
EXPLAIN SELECT * FROM users WHERE status = 'active';
```

MySQL ‡¶è‡¶∞ `EXPLAIN` command ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá query execution plan ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü ‚Äì ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® index use ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡¶ü‡¶æ slow ‡¶á‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡•§

---

<div align="center"><strong>‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ ‚ú¶ x ‚ú¶ ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ</strong></div>

# Q : What is the difference between `bind()` and `singleton()` in the service container?

Laravel-‡¶è‡¶∞ Service Container ‡¶è `bind()` ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç `singleton()` ‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶á‡¶ü‡¶æ method ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶π‡ßü dependency binding ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶ü‡¶æ mainly instance creation ‡¶è‡¶∞ behavior ‡¶®‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá‡•§


---

## üîÑ `bind()` ‡¶ï‡ßÄ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá?

`bind()` ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® service container ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶ì‡¶á class ‡¶¨‡¶æ interface ‡¶ï‡ßá resolve ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü, ‡¶§‡¶ñ‡¶® **‡¶®‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ instance ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡ßü**‡•§

```php
App::bind('App\Services\PaymentService', function ($app) {
    return new PaymentService();
});
```

> ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶®‡¶á `App::make('App\Services\PaymentService')` ‡¶¨‡¶æ constructor injection ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá call ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá, ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá object ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

üü¢ Use case:
‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶§‡ßã‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶® instance ‡¶¶‡¶∞‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶π‡ßü, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® ‚Äî user-specific ‡¶¨‡¶æ request-specific data handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

---

## üß† `singleton()` ‡¶ï‡ßÄ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá?

`singleton()` ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶•‡¶Æ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ resolve ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßü **‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ instance ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá** ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÄ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶¨ ‡¶ú‡¶æ‡ßü‡¶ó‡¶æ‡ßü **same instance ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá**‡•§

```php
App::singleton('App\Services\PaymentService', function ($app) {
    return new PaymentService();
});
```

> ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡ßé ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶á object ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶π‡ßü, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡¶¨ ‡¶ú‡¶æ‡ßü‡¶ó‡¶æ‡ßü ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶á instance ‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶∂‡ßá‡ßü‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§

üü¢ Use case:
‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶Æ‡¶ø global ‡¶¨‡¶æ shared state ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶ì, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® ‚Äî logger, config manager, cache manager, ‡¶á‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡•§

---

## üéØ ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶™‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶Ø (Summary):

| Feature     | `bind()`                               | `singleton()`                  |
| ----------- | -------------------------------------- | ------------------------------ |
| Instance    | ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶® object                  | ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø, ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ reuse  |
| Use case    | Stateless or short-living services     | Shared or long-living services |
| Performance | ‡¶ï‡¶Æ efficient (new instance every time) | ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶ø efficient (reuse)         |

---

## ‚úÖ Example Test

```php
App::singleton('Foo', function () {
    return new stdClass();
});

$one = app('Foo');
$two = app('Foo');

var_dump($one === $two); // true
```

```php
App::bind('Bar', function () {
    return new stdClass();
});

$one = app('Bar');
$two = app('Bar');

var_dump($one === $two); // false
```

---

Laravel ‡¶è‡¶∞ context ‡¶è, ‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶Æ‡¶ø ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶Æ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã class define ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßã ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ configuration ‡¶Ö‡¶•‡¶¨‡¶æ constant data ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡ßá, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá `singleton()` use ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßã‡•§ ‡¶Ü‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶Æ‡¶® class ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø request ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡ßÄ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶π‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá `bind()` better option‡•§

‡¶ö‡¶≤‡ßã, ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶® `bind()` ‡¶Ü‡¶∞ `singleton()` ‡¶è‡¶∞ **real-life practical example** ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶ø ‚Äî

---

## üßæ Real-Life Example of `singleton()`:

**Use Case**: `SettingsService` ‚Äî ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ database ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá site-wide settings (site name, logo, timezone ‡¶á‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶ø) ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ load ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç app ‡¶ú‡ßÅ‡ßú‡ßá use ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§

```php
// AppServiceProvider.php
public function register()
{
    $this->app->singleton(SettingsService::class, function ($app) {
        return new SettingsService();
    });
}
```

```php
// Anywhere in the app
$settings = app(SettingsService::class);
echo $settings->get('site_name');
```

üü¢ **Reason to use `singleton()`**: Settings ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ load ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶á app ‡¶ú‡ßÅ‡ßú‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßã‡•§ ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ query ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá performance improve ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§

---

## üõí Real-Life Example of `bind()`:

**Use Case**: `CartService` ‚Äî ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶æ user ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶Ü‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶æ shopping cart ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßü‡ßã‡¶ú‡¶®‡•§ ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶á ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø request-‡¶è ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶® instance ‡¶¶‡¶∞‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡•§

```php
// AppServiceProvider.php
public function register()
{
    $this->app->bind(CartService::class, function ($app) {
        return new CartService(auth()->user());
    });
}
```

```php
// In Controller
$cart = app(CartService::class);
$cart->add($productId);
```

üü¢ **Reason to use `bind()`**: ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø user/request ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡ßÄ ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶® cart object ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á ‚Äî ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶® user-specific cart ‡¶Ü‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶æ ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§

---

## üîÅ ‡¶ï‡¶ñ‡¶® bind(), ‡¶ï‡¶ñ‡¶® singleton()?

| Use Case                          | Method        | ‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶®?                                  |
| --------------------------------- | ------------- | ------------------------------------- |
| Site-wide config/service          | `singleton()` | ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ load ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶á ‡¶Ø‡¶•‡ßá‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü               |
| Per-user ‡¶¨‡¶æ request-based service | `bind()`      | ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø user/request ‡¶Ü‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶æ object ‡¶¶‡¶∞‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞ |

---

‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø ‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶Æ‡¶ø **CacheService, EmailService, PaymentGateway, PDF Generator** ‡¶á‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶§‡ßã service ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶ì, ‡¶§‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶á pattern ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶ñ‡ßÅ‡¶¨ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶∏‡ßá‡•§

<br>

<div align="center"><strong>‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ ‚ú¶ x ‚ú¶ ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ</strong></div>

# Q : Explain how Laravel's middleware pipeline works. How would you create and chain multiple middlewares?

Laravel-‡¶è‡¶∞ **middleware pipeline** ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ powerful mechanism, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ HTTP request ‡¶Ü‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç response ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Ü‡¶ó‡ßá ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ï‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã layer (middleware) ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶§‡¶∞ ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá pass ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶á process ‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶á middleware pipeline ‡¶¨‡¶≤‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§

---

## üß† Middleware Pipeline ‡¶ï‡ßÄ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá?

Laravel ‡¶è ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ HTTP request ‡¶Ü‡¶∏‡ßá:

1. Request ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶•‡¶Æ‡ßá `public/index.php` file ‡¶è ‡¶¢‡ßã‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§
2. ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶™‡¶∞ Kernel class (`app/Http/Kernel.php`) request ‡¶ï‡ßá handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
3. Kernel ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® middleware list ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡ßá middleware ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá request ‡¶ï‡ßá pass ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡ßü‡•§
4. ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø middleware request ‡¶ï‡ßá inspect/modify ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶¨‡¶æ next middleware ‡¶è pass ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡ßü‡•§

‡¶è‡¶á‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ middleware ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶§‡¶∞ ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá request "chain" ‡¶π‡ßü‡ßá controller ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶™‡ßå‡¶Å‡¶õ‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§

### üì§ Reverse chain:

Controller ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® response ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶π‡ßü, ‡¶§‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶†‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶ì‡¶á‡¶∏‡¶¨ middleware ‡¶Ü‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ reverse-‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá execute ‡¶π‡ßü ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶™‡¶∞ response client ‡¶è ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§

---

## üõ†Ô∏è Middleware ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡ßü‡¶Æ:

```bash
php artisan make:middleware CheckIsAdmin
```

```php
// app/Http/Middleware/CheckIsAdmin.php

public function handle($request, Closure $next)
{
    if (!auth()->check() || !auth()->user()->is_admin) {
        return redirect('/no-access');
    }

    return $next($request);
}
```

üîÅ `handle()` method-‡¶è `$next($request)` call ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá ‚Äî "‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÄ middleware ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶°‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶ì"‡•§

---

## üß© Middleware Register ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ:

```php
// app/Http/Kernel.php

protected $routeMiddleware = [
    'is_admin' => \App\Http\Middleware\CheckIsAdmin::class,
];
```

---

## üîó Multiple Middleware Chain ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ:

### ‚úÖ Route level-‡¶è:

```php
Route::get('/dashboard', function () {
    // Only for verified admin users
})->middleware(['auth', 'verified', 'is_admin']);
```

‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá,

* `auth`: Check ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá user logged in ‡¶ï‡¶ø ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§
* `verified`: Check ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá email verified ‡¶ï‡¶ø ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§
* `is_admin`: Custom middleware check ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá user admin ‡¶ï‡¶ø ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§

üëâ Middleware ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ order ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡ßÄ execute ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§

---

## üîÅ Global Middleware vs Route Middleware

| Type                  | Description                                                                               |
| --------------------- | ----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| **Global Middleware** | ‡¶∏‡¶¨ request-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø automatically apply ‡¶π‡ßü (e.g., TrimStrings, ConvertEmptyStringsToNull)‡•§ |
| **Route Middleware**  | ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü route-‡¶è apply ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§ (‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶®: `auth`, `verified`, `is_admin`)              |

---

## üéØ Bonus: Group Middleware

```php
protected $middlewareGroups = [
    'web' => [
        \App\Http\Middleware\EncryptCookies::class,
        \Illuminate\Session\Middleware\StartSession::class,
        // ‡¶Ü‡¶∞‡ßã ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ï
    ],

    'api' => [
        'throttle:api',
        \Illuminate\Routing\Middleware\SubstituteBindings::class,
    ],
];
```

---

## ‚úÖ Summary:

* Middleware ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá Laravel-‡¶è‡¶∞ request/response filtering mechanism‡•§
* Request ‚Üí Middleware 1 ‚Üí Middleware 2 ‚Üí Controller
* Controller ‚Üí Middleware 2 ‚Üí Middleware 1 ‚Üí Response
* Middleware ‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶Æ‡¶ø security, validation, logging ‡¶á‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßã‡•§
* Middleware chain ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø route-‡¶è array ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá middleware ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã define ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßã‡•§

Laravel pipeline system ‡¶ñ‡ßÅ‡¶¨ clean ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç powerful ‚Äî ‡¶è‡¶á structure ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡ßá app maintainability ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç security ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ï ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú ‡¶π‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§
